## God Nodes (most connected - your core abstractions)

2. `QuantizationConfig` - 982 edges

5. `ParallelLMHead` - 738 edges
6. `RadixAttention` - 734 edges

9. `add_prefix()` - 593 edges
10. `RMSNorm` - 547 edges

## Surprising Connections (you probably didn't know these)
- `is_prefill_only()` --calls--> `get_global_server_args()`  [INFERRED]
  managers/schedule_batch.py ↙ server_args.py
- `YieldOperation` --uses--> `ForwardBatch`  [INFERRED]
  batch_overlap/operations.py ↙ model_executor/forward_batch_info.py
- `attn_backend_wrapper()` --calls--> `import_backend_class()`  [INFERRED]
  layers/attention/attention_registry.py ↙ configs/linear_attn_model_registry.py
- `forward()` --calls--> `get_pp_group()`  [INFERRED]
  models/nemotron_nas.py ↙ distributed/parallel_state.py
- `_dequant_mlp_weight()` --calls--> `get_tensor_model_parallel_rank()`  [INFERRED]
  models/gpt_oss.py ↙ distributed/parallel_state.py
